While building the entire application here isn't feasible within our current context limit due to space constraints and complexity of such a project, I can certainly provide you with an outline for how this might be structured in Next.js.\n",
            "\n",
            "Let's say we have basic pages like Home, Product List, Product Detail, Cart, Checkout, About Us etc. Here is the basic structure:\n",
            "\n",
            "```jsx\n",
            "// Import necessary packages or modules here\n",
            "\n",
            "const Home = () => (\n",
            "  <div>\n",
            "    <h1>Welcome to our e-commerce store!</h1>\n",
            "    {/* Content goes here */}\n",
            "  </div>\n",
            ")\n",
            "\n",
            "const ProductList = ({ products }) => (\n",
            "  <div>\n",
            "    <h2>Our Products:</h2>\n",
            "    <ul>\n",
            "      {products.map(product => <li key={product.id}>{product.name}</li>)}\n",
            "    </ul>\n",
            "  </div>\n",
            ")\n",
            "\n",
            "// And so on for other pages...\n",
            "\n",
            "export default Home\n",
            "```\n",

            "\n",
            "export default function Home({ products }) {\n",
            "  const [cartItems, setCartItems] = useState([])\n",
            "\n",
            "  // Function to add a product in cart (Pseudo code)\n",
            "  function addToCart(product) {\n",
            "    setCartItems([...cartItems, product])\n",
            "  }\n",

            "  return (\n",
            "    <>\n",
            "      <Head>\n",
            "        <title>E-commerce Website</title>\n",

            "        <link rel=\"icon\" href=\"/favicon.ico\" />\n",
